- Student: Alice Brown (alice@student.examflow.pro)
- Classification: MISSING_CURRICULUM_MAPPING
- Resolution status: EXPLICITLY_ACCEPTED_UNRESOLVED
- Reason unresolved: No academic offering can be proven from the student subject tuple and current normalized group/program context.
- Recommended action: Leave the record legacy-only until historical program and group context can be reconstructed from source records.
- Candidate offerings: None
- Safe to keep unresolved: Student exam eligibility still works through the unchanged legacy tuple fields and department checks.
- Legacy fallback remains active: Student subject enrollment fallback continues to authorize legacy exam access by subject/language/group/year/semester.
- Future phase: Phase 3 historical enrollment cleanup or a dedicated data-reconstruction task must rebuild missing normalized group/program context before mapping.
- Approved by: Phase 2 completion pass on 2026-07-11
